# ğŸ§  ConRad - Adaptive AI RFP Automation System

## EY Techathon 6.0 | Revolutionizing Cable Supply RFP Discovery & Response

> **ConRad** (Contract Radar) is an intelligent, adaptive multi-agent system that completely automates the RFP (Request for Proposal) lifecycle for the cable supply industry. From discovery to bid submission, ConRad transforms a **40+ hour manual process** into a **5-minute AI-powered workflow**.

### End-to-End User Journey (Detailed)

### Agent State Management

```javascript
// LangGraph State Definition (agentic/state.js)
const AgentState = {
  // Input
  userQuery: string,
  sessionId: string,
  mode: 'SEARCH' | 'RFP_PROCEED',
  
  // Shared Context (passed between agents)
  searchResults: RFP[],
  selectedRFP: RFP | null,
  cableRequirements: CableSpec[],
  testingRequirements: Test[],
  
  // Agent Outputs
  salesOutput: { rfps: [], rankings: [] },
  technicalOutput: { matches: [], skuScores: [] },
  pricingOutput: { quotation: {}, breakdown: [] },
  submissionOutput: { package: {}, actions: [] },
  
  // Final
  consolidatedResponse: string,
  actionButtons: Button[]
}
```

## ğŸ”„ Adaptive Learning Capabilities

### How ConRad Adapts to New Data

```

### Dependencies Summary

| Category | Package | Purpose |
|----------|---------|---------|
| **Runtime** | Node.js 18+ | JavaScript runtime |
| **Framework** | Express 4.x | Web server & API |
| **AI - Primary** | @google/genai | Gemini 2.0 Flash integration |
| **AI - Fallback** | openai | OpenAI GPT-4o-mini |
| **AI - Agents** | @langchain/core | LangGraph workflow |
| **PDF Create** | pdfkit | Generate bid PDFs |
| **PDF Parse** | pdf-parse | Extract text from PDFs |
| **OCR** | @aws-sdk/client-textract | AWS Textract for scanned docs |
| **Embeddings** | @huggingface/inference | Semantic search |
| **Voice** | faster-whisper | Speech-to-text (Python) |
| **Files** | multer | File upload handling |
| **CSV** | csv-parse | CSV file processing |

---

### 3. Smart Calendar Integration

```
Natural Language Calendar Commands:

"set reminder to 2 days before"    â†’  Reminder: 2 days before due date
"reminder 1 week"                  â†’  Reminder: 7 days before
"set date to 4th jan 2027"         â†’  Event date: January 4, 2027
"change title to Urgent Deadline"  â†’  Event title updated
"add notes: bring all documents"   â†’  Notes added to calendar event

Integrates with:
â€¢ Google Calendar (via .ics file)
â€¢ Outlook Calendar
â€¢ Apple Calendar

â”‚  â”‚  Problem: RFPs have form fields that need to be identified                       â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚           e.g., "EMD Amount: â‚¹50,000" or "Due Date: 15-Jan-2026"                â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚                                                                                   â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  Solution: Textract's FORMS feature identifies key-value pairs                   â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚                                                                                   â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  Input:  Tender No.: ABC-2024-001                                                â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚          EMD Amount: â‚¹50,000                                                     â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚          Submission Date: 15-Jan-2026                                            â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚                                                                                   â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  Output: {                                                                        â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚            "Tender No.": "ABC-2024-001",                                         â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚            "EMD Amount": "â‚¹50,000",                                              â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚            "Submission Date": "15-Jan-2026"                                      â”‚   â”‚
â”‚  â”‚          }                                                                        â”‚   â”‚

### Textract vs Other Extraction Methods

| Method | Scanned PDFs | Tables | Forms | Cost |
|--------|--------------|--------|-------|------|
| **pdf-parse** | âŒ No | âŒ No | âŒ No | Free |
| **Gemini AI** | âš ï¸ Limited | âš ï¸ Limited | âœ… Yes | $0.075/1M tokens |
| **AWS Textract** | âœ… Yes | âœ… Yes | âœ… Yes | $1.50/1000 pages |

## ğŸš€ Getting Started

### Prerequisites

```
â€¢ Node.js 18+ (LTS recommended)
â€¢ Python 3.10+ (for voice service)
â€¢ npm or yarn
â€¢ Git
```

### Installation

```bash
# 1. Clone the repository
git clone https://github.com/your-repo/conrad.git
cd ConRad_Final_Submission

# 2. Install Node.js dependencies
npm install --legacy-peer-deps

# 3. Configure environment variables
cp env.txt .env
# Edit .env with your API keys:
# - GEMINI_API_KEY (required)
# - OPENAI_API_KEY (recommended)
# - AWS credentials (optional, for Textract)

# 4. Install Python dependencies for voice (optional)
pip install fastapi uvicorn python-multipart faster-whisper

# 5. Start the server
node index.js
```

### Access Points

| URL | Description |
|-----|-------------|
| http://localhost:5000/chat.html | Main AI Chat Interface |
| http://localhost:5000/ | Portal Overview |
| http://localhost:5000/agent-orchestration.html | Agent Workflow Visualization |
| http://localhost:5001/ | Voice Service (auto-started) |

---

## ğŸ“š API Reference

### Core Endpoints

| Endpoint | Method | Description |
|----------|--------|-------------|
| `/api/chat` | POST | Main chat with AI |
| `/api/ai-search/query` | POST | Search RFPs |
| `/api/rfp-proceed/analyze` | POST | Analyze specific RFP |
| `/api/rfp-proceed/generate-bid-pdf` | POST | Generate bid document |
| `/api/upload/document` | POST | Upload PDF/Word |
| `/api/adaptive-data/csv` | POST | Upload adaptive CSV |
| `/api/pdf/rfp/:tenderId` | GET | Download RFP PDF |

### Voice Endpoints (Port 5001)

| Endpoint | Method | Description |
|----------|--------|-------------|
| `/health` | GET | Health check |
| `/transcribe` | POST | Transcribe audio |

---

## ğŸ’° Cost Analysis

### API Costs (Per Month)

| Service | Free Tier | Cost if Exceeded |
|---------|-----------|------------------|
| **Gemini 2.0 Flash** | 15 RPM, 1500 RPD | $0.075/1M tokens |
| **OpenAI GPT-4o-mini** | - | $0.15/1M tokens |
| **AWS Textract** | 1000 pages/month | $1.50/1000 pages |
| **HuggingFace Embeddings** | Unlimited (local) | FREE |
| **FasterWhisper** | Unlimited (local) | FREE |

**For typical demo usage: $0 (within free tiers)**

## ğŸ“ File Structure

### Complete Project Structure

```
ConRad_Final_Submission/

â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

### Environment Variables Reference

```bash
# .env file

# Required
GEMINI_API_KEY=your_gemini_api_key           # Get from ai.google.dev

# Recommended (for fallback)
OPENAI_API_KEY=your_openai_api_key           # Get from platform.openai.com

# Optional (for AWS Textract OCR)
AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID=your_aws_access_key
AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY=your_aws_secret_key
AWS_REGION=ap-south-1

# Optional (for HuggingFace remote embeddings)
HF_API_KEY=your_huggingface_key

# Server Configuration
PORT=5000
NODE_ENV=development
```

---

## ğŸ† Key Innovations

1. **Multi-AI Fallback** - Never fails due to single provider issues
2. **Adaptive CSV Management** - Dynamic pricing without code changes
3. **Dynamic PDF Parsing** - Understands edited/modified documents
4. **Voice-First Interface** - Hands-free operation
5. **LangGraph Agents** - Intelligent task routing
6. **Real-Time Quotations** - Accurate pricing instantly
7. **4 Submission Modes** - Adapts to any RFP submission method
8. **AI Email Modification** - Natural language email editing
9. **Smart Calendar Integration** - Natural language date/reminder changes
10. **ChatGPT-Style Upload** - File + text input together
